Invalidates when content changes (different hash).\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self) -> None:\n        self._store: dict[str, FileAnalysis] = {}\n        self._stats = CacheStats()\n\n    @property\n    def stats(self) -> CacheStats:\n        return self._stats\n\n    def get(self, content_hash: str) -> FileAnalysis | None:\n        result = self._store.get(content_hash)\n        if result is not None:\n            self._stats.hits += 1\n        else:\n            self._stats.misses += 1\n        return result\n\n    def put(self, content_hash: str, result: FileAnalysis) -> None:\n        self._store[content_hash] = result\n\n    def contains(self, content_hash: str) -> bool:\n        return content_hash in self._store\n\n    def clear(self) -> None:\n        self._store.clear()\n        self._stats = CacheStats()\n\n    @property\n    def size(self) -> int:\n        return len(self._store)\n\n\ndef compute_content_hash(content: str) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Compute a SHA-256 hash of file content for cache keying.\"\"\"\n    return hashlib.sha256(content.encode(\"utf-8\")).hexdigest()\n\n\n# Type for analysis tool functions\nAnalysisTool = Callable[[str, str], FileAnalysis]\n\n\ndef _default_analyzer(file_path: str, content: str) -> FileAnalysis:\n    \"\"\"Default static analyzer: extracts basic import/export patterns.\n\n    This is a simple line-based scanner. In production, AST-based\n    analysis would be plugged in via the tool parameter.\n    \"\"\"\n    lines = content.splitlines()\n    imports: list[str] = []\n    exports: list[str] = []\n\n    for line in lines:\n        stripped = line.strip()\n        # Python imports\n        if stripped.startswith(\"import \") or stripped.startswith(\"from \"):\n            imports.append(stripped)\n        # JS/TS imports\n        elif stripped.startswith(\"import \"):\n            imports.append(stripped)\n        # Python __all__\n        elif \"__all__\" in stripped:\n            exports.append(stripped)\n        # JS/TS exports\n        elif stripped.startswith(\"export \"):\n            exports.append(stripped)\n\n    return FileAnalysis(\n        file_path=file_path,\n        content_hash=compute_content_hash(content),\n        imports=imports,\n        exports=exports,\n        references=[],\n        metadata={\n            \"line_count\": len(lines),\n            \"size_bytes\": len(content),\n        },\n    )\n\n\nclass ToolOrchestrator:\n    \"\"\"Orchestrates static analysis tools per batch with caching.\n\n    Dispatches analysis for each file, using cached results when\n    content hasn't changed. Tracks cache statistics.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(\n        self,\n        analyzer: AnalysisTool | None = None,\n        cache: ResultCache | None = None,\n    ) -> None:\n        self._analyzer = analyzer or _default_analyzer\n        self._cache = cache or ResultCache()\n\n    @property\n    def cache(self) -> ResultCache:\n        return self._cache\n\n    def analyze_file(self, file_path: str, content: str) -> FileAnalysis:\n        \"\"\"Analyze a single file, using cache when possible.\"\"\"\n        content_hash = compute_content_hash(content)\n\n        cached = self._cache.get(content_hash)\n        if cached is not None:\n            return cached\n\n        result = self._analyzer(file_path, content)\n        self._cache.put(content_hash, result)\n        return result\n\n    def analyze_batch(\n        self,\n        files: dict[str, str],\n    ) -> list[FileAnalysis]:\n        \"\"\"Analyze a batch of files (path -> content mapping).\n\n        Returns list of FileAnalysis results. Uses cache for unchanged files.\n        \"\"\"\n        results = []\n        for file_path, content in files.items():\n            result = self.analyze_file(file_path, content)\n            results.append(result)\n        return results\n\n    def get_cache_stats(self) -> CacheStats:\n        return self._cache.stats\n","numLines":193,"startLine":1,"totalLines":193}}}

isinstance(annotation, ast.Subscript):\n   236→        if isinstance(annotation.value, ast.Name) and annotation.value.id == \"Optional\":\n   237→            slice_val = annotation.slice\n   238→            if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Name) and slice_val.id == \"Callable\":\n   239→                return True\n   240→            # Optional[Callable[...]]\n   241→            if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Subscript):\n   242→                if isinstance(slice_val.value, ast.Name) and slice_val.value.id == \"Callable\":\n   243→                    return True\n   244→        # Also check Attribute form: typing.Optional\n   245→        if isinstance(annotation.value, ast.Attribute):\n   246→            if annotation.value.attr == \"Optional\":\n   247→                slice_val = annotation.slice\n   248→                if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Name) and slice_val.id == \"Callable\":\n   249→                    return True\n   250→\n   251→    # Callable | None -> BinOp(Name('Callable'), BitOr, Constant(None))\n   252→    if isinstance(annotation, ast.BinOp) and isinstance(annotation.op, ast.BitOr):\n   253→        left, right = annotation.left, annotation.right\n   254→        if (isinstance(left, ast.Name) and left.id == \"Callable\" and\n   255→                isinstance(right, ast.Constant) and right.value is None):\n   256→            return True\n   257→        if (isinstance(right, ast.Name) and right.id == \"Callable\" and\n   258→                isinstance(left, ast.Constant) and left.value is None):\n   259→            return True\n   260→\n   261→    return False\n   262→\n   263→\n   264→def _has_none_default(func_def: ast.FunctionDef, target_arg: ast.arg) -> bool:\n   265→    \"\"\"Check if the given arg has a default value of None.\"\"\"\n   266→    args = func_def.args\n   267→    # defaults apply to the last N positional args\n   268→    all_args = args.args\n   269→    defaults = args.defaults\n   270→\n   271→    if not defaults:\n   272→        return False\n   273→\n   274→    # Map defaults to args (right-aligned)\n   275→    offset = len(all_args) - len(defaults)\n   276→    for i, arg in enumerate(all_args):\n   277→        if arg is target_arg:\n   278→            default_idx = i - offset\n   279→            if 0 <= default_idx < len(defaults):\n   280→                default = defaults[default_idx]\n   281→                return isinstance(default, ast.Constant) and default.value is None\n   282→    return False\n   283→\n   284→\n   285→def _find_wiring_call_sites(\n   286→    param_name: str,\n   287→    class_name: str,\n   288→    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module],\n   289→) -> bool:\n   290→    \"\"\"Search for call sites that explicitly provide the parameter by keyword.\"\"\"\n   291→    for tree in trees.values():\n   292→        for node in ast.walk(tree):\n   293→            if isinstance(node, ast.Call):\n   294→                # Check keyword arguments\n   295→                for kw in node.keywords:\n   296→                    if kw.arg == param_name:\n   297→                        # Verify it's calling the right class\n   298→                        if _is_class_call(node, class_name):\n   299→                            return True\n   300→    return False\n   301→\n   302→\n   303→def _is_class_call(call: ast.Call, class_name: str) -> bool:\n   304→    \"\"\"Check if a Call node is calling the specified class.\"\"\"\n   305→    func = call.func\n   306→    if isinstance(func, ast.Name) and func.id == class_name:\n   307→        return True\n   308→    if isinstance(func, ast.Attribute) and func.attr == class_name:\n   309→        return True\n   310→    return False\n   311→\n   312→\n   313→def analyze_unwired_callables(\n   314→    config: WiringConfig,\n   315→    source_dir: Path,\n   316→) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n   317→    \"\"\"Detect injectable callables (Optional[Callable]) that are never wired.\n   318→\n   319→    Algorithm (section 5.2.1):\n   320→    1. Parse all Python files, extract Optional[Callable] constructor params\n   321→    2. For each injectable, search all files for keyword call sites\n   322→    3. If zero providers, emit unwired_callable finding\n   323→    4. Apply whitelist suppression\n   324→\n   325→    Args:\n   326→        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n   327→        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n   328→\n   329→    Returns:\n   330→        List of WiringFinding with finding_type=\"unwired_callable\".\n   331→    \"\"\"\n   332→    files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n   333→    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module] = {}\n   334→\n   335→    for f in files:\n   336→        tree = _safe_parse(f)\n   337→        if tree is not None:\n   338→            trees[f] = tree\n   339→\n   340→    findings: list[WiringFinding] = []\n   341→\n   342→    for file_path, tree in trees.items():\n   343→        injectables = _extract_injectable_params(tree, str(file_path))\n   344→        for symbol, param_name, lineno in injectables:\n   345→            class_name = symbol.split(\".\")[0]\n   346→            if not _find_wiring_call_sites(param_name, class_name, trees):\n   347→                findings.append(\n   348→                    WiringFinding(\n   349→                        finding_type=\"unwired_callable\",\n   350→                        file_path=str(file_path),\n   351→                        symbol_name=symbol,\n   352→                        line_number=lineno,\n   353→                        detail=(\n   354→                            f\"Parameter '{param_name}' typed Optional[Callable] \"\n   355→                            f\"with default None is never wired by any call site\"\n   356→                        ),\n   357→                        severity=\"critical\",\n   358→                    )\n   359→                )\n   360→\n   361→    # Apply whitelist\n   362→    whitelist = load_whitelist(config.whitelist_path, config.rollout_mode)\n   363→    return _apply_whitelist(findings, whitelist)\n   364→\n   365→\n   366→# --- G-002: Orphan Module Analysis (section 5.2.2) ---\n   367→\n   368→\n   369→def _find_provider_dirs(source_dir: Path, provider_names: frozenset[str]) -> list[Path]:\n   370→    \"\"\"Find directories matching provider_dir_names convention.\"\"\"\n   371→    providers: list[Path] = []\n   372→    for d in sorted(source_dir.rglob(\"*\")):\n   373→        if d.is_dir() and d.name in provider_names:\n   374→            providers.append(d)\n   375→    return providers\n   376→\n   377→\n   378→def _extract_imports(tree: ast.Module) -> set[str]:\n   379→    \"\"\"Extract all imported module/symbol names from an AST.\"\"\"\n   380→    imports: set[str] = set()\n   381→    for node in ast.walk(tree):\n   382→        if isinstance(node, ast.Import):\n   383→            for alias in node.names:\n   384→                imports.add(alias.name)\n   385→        elif isinstance(node, ast.ImportFrom):\n   386→            if node.module:\n   387→                imports.add(node.module)\n   388→                for alias in node.names:\n   389→                    imports.add(f\"{node.module}.{alias.name}\")\n   390→    return imports\n   391→\n   392→\n   393→def analyze_orphan_modules(\n   394→    config: WiringConfig,\n   395→    source_dir: Path,\n   396→) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n   397→    \"\"\"Detect Python modules in provider directories with zero inbound imports.\n   398→\n   399→    Algorithm (section 5.2.2):\n   400→    1. Find provider directories by config.provider_dir_names convention\n   401→    2. For each Python file in provider dirs, check if any file outside\n   402→       the provider dir imports it\n   403→    3. If zero importers, emit orphan_module finding\n   404→    4. Apply exclude_patterns and whitelist suppression\n   405→\n   406→    Args:\n   407→        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n   408→        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n   409→\n   410→    Returns:\n   411→        List of WiringFinding with finding_type=\"orphan_module\".\n   412→    \"\"\"\n   413→    provider_dirs = _find_provider_dirs(source_dir, config.provider_dir_names)\n   414→    if not provider_dirs:\n   415→        return []\n   416→\n   417→    # Collect all Python files and parse them for imports\n   418→    all_files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, [])\n   419→    all_imports: set[str] = set()\n   420→    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module] = {}\n   421→\n   422→    for f in all_files:\n   423→        tree = _safe_parse(f)\n   424→        if tree is not None:\n   425→            trees[f] = tree\n   426→\n   427→    # Gather imports from files OUTSIDE provider directories\n   428→    for f, tree in trees.items():\n   429→        is_in_provider = any(\n   430→            f.resolve().is_relative_to(pd.resolve()) for pd in provider_dirs\n   431→        )\n   432→        if not is_in_provider:\n   433→            all_imports.update(_extract_imports(tree))\n   434→\n   435→    findings: list[WiringFinding] = []\n   436→\n   437→    for provider_dir in provider_dirs:\n   438→        for py_file in sorted(provider_dir.glob(\"*.py\")):\n   439→            # Apply exclude patterns\n   440→            if any(fnmatch(py_file.name, pat) for pat in config.exclude_patterns):\n   441→                continue\n   442→\n   443→            # Derive the module path components\n   444→            try:\n   445→                rel = py_file.relative_to(source_dir)\n   446→            except ValueError:\n   447→                continue\n   448→\n   449→            # Build possible import names\n   450→            module_stem = py_file.stem\n   451→            module_dotpath = str(rel.with_suffix(\"\")).replace(\"/\", \".\").replace(\"\\\\\", \".\")\n   452→\n   453→            # Check if any external file imports this module\n   454→            is_imported = False\n   455→            for imp in all_imports:\n   456→                if module_dotpath in imp or module_stem in imp:\n   457→                    is_imported = True\n   458→                    break\n   459→\n   460→            if not is_imported:\n   461→                findings.append(\n   462→                    WiringFinding(\n   463→                        finding_type=\"orphan_module\",\n   464→                        file_path=str(py_file),\n   465→                        symbol_name=module_dotpath,\n   466→                        line_number=1,\n   467→                        detail=(\n   468→                            f\"Module '{module_dotpath}' in provider directory \"\n   469→                            f\"'{provider_dir.name}' has zero inbound imports\"\n   470→                        ),\n   471→                        severity=\"major\",\n   472→                    )\n   473→                )\n   474→\n   475→    # Apply whitelist\n   476→    whitelist = load_whitelist(config.whitelist_path, config.rollout_mode)\n   477→    return _apply_whitelist(findings, whitelist)\n   478→\n   479→\n   480→# --- G-003: Registry Analysis (section 5.2.3) ---\n   481→\n   482→\n   483→def _matches_registry_pattern(\n   484→    name: str, patterns: tuple[re.Pattern[str], ...]\n   485→) -> bool:\n   486→    \"\"\"Check if a variable name matches any registry detection pattern.\"\"\"\n   487→    return any(p.match(name) for p in patterns)\n   488→\n   489→\n   490→def _resolve_name_in_scope(\n   491→    name: str, tree: ast.Module, all_imports: set[str]\n   492→) -> bool:\n   493→    \"\"\"Check if a name is resolvable: defined in module or importable.\"\"\"\n   494→    # Check module-level definitions\n   495→    for node in ast.iter_child_nodes(tree):\n   496→        if isinstance(node, (ast.FunctionDef, ast.AsyncFunctionDef)):\n   497→            if node.name == name:\n   498→                return True\n   499→        elif isinstance(node, ast.ClassDef):\n   500→            if node.name == name:\n   501→                return True\n   502→        elif isinstance(node, ast.Assign):\n   503→            for target in node.targets:\n   504→                if isinstance(target, ast.Name) and target.id == name:\n   505→                    return True\n   506→\n   507→    # Check if importable\n   508→    if name in all_imports:\n   509→        return True\n   510→\n   511→    return False\n   512→\n   513→\n   514→def analyze_registries(\n   515→    config: WiringConfig,\n   516→    source_dir: Path,\n   517→) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n   518→    \"\"\"Detect broken dispatch registry entries referencing nonexistent callables.\n   519→\n   520→    Algorithm (section 5.2.3):\n   521→    1. Scan files for module-level dict assignments matching registry patterns\n   522→    2. For each dict entry, verify the value references an importable callable\n   523→    3. Unresolved references emit unwired_registry findings\n   524→\n   525→    Args:\n   526→        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n   527→        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n   528→\n   529→    Returns:\n   530→        List of WiringFinding with finding_type=\"unwired_registry\".\n   531→    \"\"\"\n   532→    files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n   533→    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module] = {}\n   534→    all_imports_by_file: dict[Path, set[str]] = {}\n   535→\n   536→    for f in files:\n   537→        tree = _safe_parse(f)\n   538→        if tree is not None:\n   539→            trees[f] = tree\n   540→            all_imports_by_file[f] = _extract_imports(tree)\n   541→\n   542→    findings: list[WiringFinding] = []\n   543→\n   544→    for file_path, tree in trees.items():\n   545→        file_imports = all_imports_by_file.get(file_path, set())\n   546→\n   547→        for node in ast.iter_child_nodes(tree):\n   548→            if not isinstance(node, ast.Assign):\n   549→                continue\n   550→\n   551→            for target in node.targets:\n   552→                if not isinstance(target, ast.Name):\n   553→                    continue\n   554→                if not _matches_registry_pattern(target.id, config.registry_patterns):\n   555→                    continue\n   556→\n   557→                # This is a registry assignment — check if value is a dict\n   558→                if not isinstance(node.value, ast.Dict):\n   559→                    continue\n   560→\n   561→                for key_node, val_node in zip(node.value.keys, node.value.values):\n   562→                    if val_node is None:\n   563→                        continue\n   564→\n   565→                    # Explicit None is allowed\n   566→                    if isinstance(val_node, ast.Constant) and val_node.value is None:\n   567→                        continue\n   568→\n   569→                    # Name reference — must be resolvable\n   570→                    if isinstance(val_node, ast.Name):\n   571→                        if not _resolve_name_in_scope(\n   572→                            val_node.id, tree, file_imports\n   573→                        ):\n   574→                            key_repr = (\n   575→                                ast.literal_eval(key_node)\n   576→                                if isinstance(key_node, ast.Constant)\n   577→                                else \"<dynamic>\"\n   578→                            )\n   579→                            findings.append(\n   580→                                WiringFinding(\n   581→                                    finding_type=\"unwired_registry\",\n   582→                                    file_path=str(file_path),\n   583→                                    symbol_name=f\"{target.id}[{key_repr!r}]\",\n   584→                                    line_number=val_node.lineno,\n   585→                                    detail=(\n   586→                                        f\"Registry '{target.id}' entry \"\n   587→                                        f\"'{key_repr}' references unresolvable \"\n   588→                                        f\"callable '{val_node.id}'\"\n   589→                                    ),\n   590→                                    severity=\"critical\",\n   591→                                )\n   592→                            )\n   593→\n   594→                    # String reference — try to resolve as dotted path\n   595→                    elif isinstance(val_node, ast.Constant) and isinstance(\n   596→                        val_node.value, str\n   597→                    ):\n   598→                        ref = val_node.value\n   599→                        parts = ref.rsplit(\".\", 1)\n   600→                        func_name = parts[-1] if len(parts) > 1 else ref\n   601→                        if not _resolve_name_in_scope(\n   602→                            func_name, tree, file_imports\n   603→                        ):\n   604→                            key_repr = (\n   605→                                ast.literal_eval(key_node)\n   606→                                if isinstance(key_node, ast.Constant)\n   607→                                else \"<dynamic>\"\n   608→                            )\n   609→                            findings.append(\n   610→                                WiringFinding(\n   611→                                    finding_type=\"unwired_registry\",\n   612→                                    file_path=str(file_path),\n   613→                                    symbol_name=f\"{target.id}[{key_repr!r}]\",\n   614→                                    line_number=val_node.lineno,\n   615→                                    detail=(\n   616→                                        f\"Registry '{target.id}' entry \"\n   617→                                        f\"'{key_repr}' references unresolvable \"\n   618→                                        f\"string path '{ref}'\"\n   619→                                    ),\n   620→                                    severity=\"critical\",\n   621→                                )\n   622→                            )\n   623→\n   624→    # Apply whitelist\n   625→    whitelist = load_whitelist(config.whitelist_path, config.rollout_mode)\n   626→    return _apply_whitelist(findings, whitelist)\n   627→\n   628→\n   629→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   630→# Top-level entry point\n   631→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   632→\n   633→\n   634→def run_wiring_analysis(\n   635→    config: WiringConfig,\n   636→    source_dir: Path,\n   637→) -> WiringReport:\n   638→    \"\"\"Run all three wiring analyzers and produce a WiringReport.\n   639→\n   640→    Args:\n   641→        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n   642→        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n   643→\n   644→    Returns:\n   645→        WiringReport aggregating findings from all analyzers.\n   646→    \"\"\"\n   647→    start = time.monotonic()\n   648→\n   649→    _, skipped = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n   650→    files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n   651→    files_analyzed = len(files)\n   652→\n   653→    unwired = analyze_unwired_callables(config, source_dir)\n   654→    orphans = analyze_orphan_modules(config, source_dir)\n   655→    registries = analyze_registries(config, source_dir)\n   656→\n   657→    duration = time.monotonic() - start\n   658→\n   659→    return WiringReport(\n   660→        target_dir=str(source_dir),\n   661→        files_analyzed=files_analyzed,\n   662→        files_skipped=skipped,\n   663→        unwired_callables=unwired,\n   664→        orphan_modules=orphans,\n   665→        unwired_registries=registries,\n   666→        scan_duration_seconds=round(duration, 4),\n   667→        rollout_mode=config.rollout_mode,\n   668→    )\n   669→\n   670→\n   671→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   672→# Report emission (section 5.4)\n   673→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   674→\n   675→\n   676→def emit_report(report: WiringReport, output_path: Path) -> Path:\n   677→    \"\"\"Write a wiring verification report with YAML frontmatter and 7 Markdown sections.\n   678→\n   679→    Frontmatter contains 16 fields per section 5.6. String fields are serialized\n   680→    with yaml.safe_dump() to prevent YAML injection (section 5.4).\n   681→\n   682→    Args:\n   683→        report: Aggregated wiring analysis report.\n   684→        output_path: Destination file path.\n   685→\n   686→    Returns:\n   687→        The output_path after writing.\n   688→    \"\"\"\n   689→    # Compute severity counts from unsuppressed findings\n   690→    unsuppressed = report.unsuppressed_findings\n   691→    critical_count = sum(1 for f in unsuppressed if f.severity == \"critical\")\n   692→    major_count = sum(1 for f in unsuppressed if f.severity == \"major\")\n   693→    info_count = sum(1 for f in unsuppressed if f.severity == \"info\")\n   694→    suppressed_count = sum(1 for f in report.all_findings if f.suppressed)\n   695→\n   696→    # blocking_findings depends on rollout_mode\n   697→    blocking = report.blocking_count()\n   698→\n   699→    # Build frontmatter dict (16 fields per section 5.6)\n   700→    fm: dict = {\n   701→        \"gate\": \"wiring-verification\",\n   702→        \"target_dir\": report.target_dir,\n   703→        \"files_analyzed\": report.files_analyzed,\n   704→        \"files_skipped\": report.files_skipped,\n   705→        \"rollout_mode\": report.rollout_mode,\n   706→        \"analysis_complete\": True,\n   707→        \"audit_artifacts_used\": 0,\n   708→        \"unwired_callable_count\": len([\n   709→            f for f in report.unwired_callables if not f.suppressed\n   710→        ]),\n   711→        \"orphan_module_count\": len([\n   712→            f for f in report.orphan_modules if not f.suppressed\n   713→        ]),\n   714→        \"unwired_registry_count\": len([\n   715→            f for f in report.unwired_registries if not f.suppressed\n   716→        ]),\n   717→        \"critical_count\": critical_count,\n   718→        \"major_count\": major_count,\n   719→        \"info_count\": info_count,\n   720→        \"total_findings\": len(unsuppressed),\n   721→        \"blocking_findings\": blocking,\n   722→        \"whitelist_entries_applied\": suppressed_count,\n   723→    }\n   724→\n   725→    # Serialize frontmatter with yaml.safe_dump for string safety\n   726→    fm_yaml = yaml.safe_dump(fm, default_flow_style=False, sort_keys=False)\n   727→\n   728→    # Build Markdown body with 7 sections (section 5.4.1)\n   729→    sections: list[str] = []\n   730→\n   731→    # 1. Summary\n   732→    sections.append(\"## Summary\\n\")\n   733→    sections.append(\n   734→        f\"- **Target**: {report.target_dir}\\n\"\n   735→        f\"- **Files analyzed**: {report.files_analyzed}\\n\"\n   736→        f\"- **Files skipped**: {report.files_skipped}\\n\"\n   737→        f\"- **Rollout mode**: {report.rollout_mode}\\n\"\n   738→        f\"- **Total findings**: {len(unsuppressed)}\\n\"\n   739→        f\"- **Blocking findings**: {blocking}\\n\"\n   740→        f\"- **Scan duration**: {report.scan_duration_seconds:.4f}s\\n\"\n   741→    )\n   742→\n   743→    # 2. Unwired Optional Callable Injections\n   744→    sections.append(\"## Unwired Optional Callable Injections\\n\")\n   745→    uc = [f for f in report.unwired_callables if not f.suppressed]\n   746→    if uc:\n   747→        for f in uc:\n   748→            sections.append(\n   749→                f\"- **{f.symbol_name}** ({f.file_path}:{f.line_number}) \"\n   750→                f\"[{f.severity}]: {f.detail}\\n\"\n   751→            )\n   752→    else:\n   753→        sections.append(\"No unsuppressed unwired callable findings.\\n\")\n   754→\n   755→    # 3. Orphan Modules / Symbols\n   756→    sections.append(\"## Orphan Modules / Symbols\\n\")\n   757→    om = [f for f in report.orphan_modules if not f.suppressed]\n   758→    if om:\n   759→        for f in om:\n   760→            sections.append(\n   761→                f\"- **{f.symbol_name}** ({f.file_path}:{f.line_number}) \"\n   762→                f\"[{f.severity}]: {f.detail}\\n\"\n   763→            )\n   764→    else:\n   765→        sections.append(\"No unsuppressed orphan module findings.\\n\")\n   766→\n   767→    # 4. Unregistered Dispatch Entries\n   768→    sections.append(\"## Unregistered Dispatch Entries\\n\")\n   769→    ur = [f for f in report.unwired_registries if not f.suppressed]\n   770→    if ur:\n   771→        for f in ur:\n   772→            sections.append(\n   773→                f\"- **{f.symbol_name}** ({f.file_path}:{f.line_number}) \"\n   774→                f\"[{f.severity}]: {f.detail}\\n\"\n   775→            )\n   776→    else:\n   777→        sections.append(\"No unsuppressed registry findings.\\n\")\n   778→\n   779→    # 5. Suppressions and Dynamic Retention\n   780→    sections.append(\"## Suppressions and Dynamic Retention\\n\")\n   781→    suppressed_findings = [f for f in report.all_findings if f.suppressed]\n   782→    if suppressed_findings:\n   783→        for f in suppressed_findings:\n   784→            sections.append(\n   785→                f\"- **{f.symbol_name}** ({f.finding_type}): suppressed\\n\"\n   786→            )\n   787→    else:\n   788→        sections.append(\"No suppressions applied.\\n\")\n   789→    sections.append(f\"- Audit artifacts used: 0\\n\")\n   790→\n   791→    # 6. Recommended Remediation\n   792→    sections.append(\"## Recommended Remediation\\n\")\n   793→    if uc:\n   794→        sections.append(\n   795→            \"- **Unwired callables**: Wire Optional[Callable] parameters \"\n   796→            \"at call sites or add to whitelist if intentionally unused.\\n\"\n   797→        )\n   798→    if om:\n   799→        sections.append(\n   800→            \"- **Orphan modules**: Import orphan modules from consumer code \"\n   801→            \"or remove if no longer needed.\\n\"\n   802→        )\n   803→    if ur:\n   804→        sections.append(\n   805→            \"- **Broken registries**: Fix registry entries to reference \"\n   806→            \"resolvable callables or remove stale entries.\\n\"\n   807→        )\n   808→    if not uc and not om and not ur:\n   809→        sections.append(\"No remediation needed — all checks pass.\\n\")\n   810→\n   811→    # 7.                         (symbol, arg.arg, arg.lineno)\n                        )\n\n    return injectables\n\n\ndef _is_optional_callable(annotation: ast.expr) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if an annotation represents Optional[Callable] or Callable | None.\"\"\"\n    # Optional[Callable] -> Subscript(Name('Optional'), Name('Callable'))\n    if isinstance(annotation, ast.Subscript):\n        if isinstance(annotation.value, ast.Name) and annotation.value.id == \"Optional\":\n            slice_val = annotation.slice\n            if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Name) and slice_val.id == \"Callable\":\n                return True\n            # Optional[Callable[...]]\n            if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Subscript):\n                if isinstance(slice_val.value, ast.Name) and slice_val.value.id == \"Callable\":\n                    return True\n        # Also check Attribute form: typing.Optional\n        if isinstance(annotation.value, ast.Attribute):\n            if annotation.value.attr == \"Optional\":\n                slice_val = annotation.slice\n                if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Name) and slice_val.id == \"Callable\":\n                    return annotation.left, annotation.right\n        if (isinstance(left, ast.Name) and left.id == \"Callable\" and\n                isinstance(right, ast.Constant) and right.value is None):\n            return class_name:\n        return True\n    if isinstance(func, ast.Attribute) and func.attr == class_name:\n        return True\n    return False\n\n\ndef analyze_unwired_callables(\n    config: If zero providers, emit unwired_callable finding\n    4. Gather imports from files OUTSIDE provider directories\n    for f, tree in trees.items():\n        is_in_provider = any(\n            f.resolve().is_relative_to(pd.resolve()) for pd in provider_dirs\n        )\n        if not is_in_provider:\n            all_imports.update(_extract_imports(tree))\n\n    findings: list[WiringFinding] = []\n\n    for provider_dir in provider_dirs:\n        for py_file in sorted(provider_dir.glob(\"*.py\")):\n            # Build possible import names\n            module_stem = py_file.stem\n            module_dotpath = str(rel.with_suffix(\"\")).replace(\"/\", \".\").replace(\"\\\\\", \".\")\n\n            # Check if any external file imports this module\n            is_imported = False\n            for imp in all_imports:\n                if module_dotpath in imp or module_stem in imp:\n                    is_imported = True\n                    break\n\n            if not is_imported:\n                findings.append(\n                    WiringFinding(\n                        finding_type=\"orphan_module\",\n                        file_path=str(py_file),\n                        symbol_name=module_dotpath,\n                        line_number=1,\n                        detail=(\n                            f\"Module '{module_dotpath}' in provider directory \"\n                            f\"'{provider_dir.name}' has zero inbound imports\"\n                        ),\n                        severity=\"major\",\n                    )\n                )\n\n    # Apply whitelist\n    whitelist = load_whitelist(config.whitelist_path, config.rollout_mode)\n    return _apply_whitelist(findings, whitelist)\n\n\n# --- G-003: Registry Analysis (section 5.2.3) ---\n\n\ndef _matches_registry_pattern(\n    name: str, patterns: tuple[re.Pattern[str], ...]\n) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if a variable name matches any registry detection pattern.\"\"\"\n    return any(p.match(name) for p in patterns)\n\n\ndef _resolve_name_in_scope(\n    name: str, tree: ast.Module, all_imports: set[str]\n) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if a name is resolvable: defined in module or importable.\"\"\"\n    # Check module-level definitions\n    for node in ast.iter_child_nodes(tree):\n        if isinstance(node, (ast.FunctionDef, ast.AsyncFunctionDef)):\n            if node.name == name:\n                return True\n        elif isinstance(node, ast.ClassDef):\n            if node.name == name:\n                return True\n        elif isinstance(node, ast.Assign):\n            for target in node.targets:\n                if isinstance(target, ast.Name) and target.id == name:\n                    return True\n\n    # Check if importable\n    if name in all_imports:\n        return True\n\n    return False\n\n\ndef analyze_registries(\n    config: WiringConfig,\n    source_dir: Path,\n) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n    \"\"\"Detect broken dispatch registry entries referencing nonexistent callables.\n\n    Algorithm (section 5.2.3):\n    1. Scan files for module-level dict assignments matching registry patterns\n    2. For each dict entry, verify the value references an importable callable\n    3. Unresolved references emit unwired_registry findings\n\n    Args:\n        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n\n    Returns:\n        List of WiringFinding with finding_type=\"unwired_registry\".\n    \"\"\"\n    files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module] = {}\n    all_imports_by_file: dict[Path, set[str]] = {}\n\n    for f in files:\n        tree = _safe_parse(f)\n        if tree is not None:\n            trees[f] = tree\n            all_imports_by_file[f] = _extract_imports(tree)\n\n    findings: list[WiringFinding] = []\n\n    for file_path, tree in trees.items():\n        file_imports = all_imports_by_file.get(file_path, set())\n\n        for node in ast.iter_child_nodes(tree):\n            if not isinstance(node, ast.Assign):\n                continue\n\n            for target in node.targets:\n                if not isinstance(target, ast.Name):\n                    continue\n                if not _matches_registry_pattern(target.id, config.registry_patterns):\n                    continue\n\n                # This is a registry assignment — check if value is a dict\n                if not isinstance(node.value, ast.Dict):\n                    continue\n\n                for key_node, val_node in zip(node.value.keys, node.value.values):\n                    if val_node is None:\n                        continue\n\n                    # Explicit None is allowed\n                    if isinstance(val_node, ast.Constant) and val_node.value is None:\n                        continue\n\n                    # Name reference — must be resolvable\n                    if isinstance(val_node, ast.Name):\n                        if not _resolve_name_in_scope(\n                            val_node.id, tree, file_imports\n                        ):\n                            key_repr = (\n                                ast.literal_eval(key_node)\n                                if isinstance(key_node, ast.Constant)\n                                else \"<dynamic>\"\n                            )\n                            findings.append(\n                                WiringFinding(\n                                    finding_type=\"unwired_registry\",\n                                    file_path=str(file_path),\n                                    symbol_name=f\"{target.id}[{key_repr!r}]\",\n                                    line_number=val_node.lineno,\n                                    detail=(\n                                        f\"Registry '{target.id}' entry \"\n                                        f\"'{key_repr}' references unresolvable \"\n                                        f\"callable '{val_node.id}'\"\n                                    ),\n                                    severity=\"critical\",\n                                )\n                            )\n\n                    # String reference — try to resolve as dotted path\n                    elif isinstance(val_node, ast.Constant) and isinstance(\n                        val_node.value, str\n                    ):\n                        ref = val_node.value\n                        parts = ref.rsplit(\".\", 1)\n                        func_name = parts[-1] if len(parts) > 1 else ref\n                        if not _resolve_name_in_scope(\n                            func_name, tree, file_imports\n                        ):\n                            key_repr = (\n                                ast.literal_eval(key_node)\n                                if isinstance(key_node, ast.Constant)\n                                else \"<dynamic>\"\n                            )\n                            findings.append(\n                                WiringFinding(\n                                    finding_type=\"unwired_registry\",\n                                    file_path=str(file_path),\n                                    symbol_name=f\"{target.id}[{key_repr!r}]\",\n                                    line_number=val_node.lineno,\n                                    detail=(\n                                        f\"Registry '{target.id}' entry \"\n                                        f\"'{key_repr}' references unresolvable \"\n                                        f\"string path '{ref}'\"\n                                    ),\n                                    severity=\"critical\",\n                                )\n                            )\n\n    # Apply whitelist\n    whitelist = load_whitelist(config.whitelist_path, config.rollout_mode)\n    return _apply_whitelist(findings, whitelist)\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Top-level entry point\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef run_wiring_analysis(\n    config: WiringConfig,\n    source_dir: Path,\n) -> WiringReport:\n    \"\"\"Run all three wiring analyzers and produce a WiringReport.\n\n    Args:\n        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n\n    Returns:\n        WiringReport aggregating findings from all analyzers.\n    \"\"\"\n    start = time.monotonic()\n\n    _, skipped = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n    files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n    files_analyzed = len(files)\n\n    unwired = analyze_unwired_callables(config, source_dir)\n    orphans = analyze_orphan_modules(config, source_dir)\n    registries = analyze_registries(config, source_dir)\n\n    duration = time.monotonic() - start\n\n    return WiringReport(\n        target_dir=str(source_dir),\n        files_analyzed=files_analyzed,\n        files_skipped=skipped,\n        unwired_callables=unwired,\n        orphan_modules=orphans,\n        unwired_registries=registries,\n        scan_duration_seconds=round(duration, 4),\n        rollout_mode=config.rollout_mode,\n    )\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Report emission (section 5.4)\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef emit_report(report: WiringReport, output_path: Path) -> Path:\n    \"\"\"Write a wiring verification report with YAML frontmatter and 7 Markdown sections.\n\n    Frontmatter contains 16 fields per section 5.6. String fields are serialized\n    with yaml.safe_dump() to prevent YAML injection (section 5.4).\n\n    Args:\n        report: Aggregated wiring analysis report.\n        output_path: Destination file path.\n\n    Returns:\n        The output_path after writing.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Compute severity counts from unsuppressed findings\n    unsuppressed = report.unsuppressed_findings\n    critical_count = sum(1 for f in unsuppressed if f.severity == \"critical\")\n    major_count = sum(1 for f in unsuppressed if f.severity == \"major\")\n    info_count = sum(1 for f in unsuppressed if f.severity == \"info\")\n    suppressed_count = sum(1 for f in report.all_findings if f.suppressed)\n\n    # blocking_findings depends on rollout_mode\n    blocking = report.blocking_count()\n\n    # Build frontmatter dict (16 fields per section 5.6)\n    fm: dict = {\n        \"gate\": \"wiring-verification\",\n        \"target_dir\": report.target_dir,\n        \"files_analyzed\": report.files_analyzed,\n        \"files_skipped\": report.files_skipped,\n        \"rollout_mode\": report.rollout_mode,\n        \"analysis_complete\": True,\n        \"audit_artifacts_used\": 0,\n        \"unwired_callable_count\": len([\n            f for f in report.unwired_callables if not f.suppressed\n        ]),\n        \"orphan_module_count\": len([\n            f for f in report.orphan_modules if not f.suppressed\n        ]),\n        \"unwired_registry_count\": len([\n            f for f in report.unwired_registries if not f.suppressed\n        ]),\n        \"critical_count\": critical_count,\n        \"major_count\": major_count,\n        \"info_count\": info_count,\n        \"total_findings\": len(unsuppressed),\n        \"blocking_findings\": blocking,\n        \"whitelist_entries_applied\": suppressed_count,\n    }\n\n    # Serialize frontmatter with yaml.safe_dump for string safety\n    fm_yaml = yaml.safe_dump(fm, default_flow_style=False, sort_keys=False)\n\n    # Build Markdown body with 7 sections (section 5.4.1)\n    sections: list[str] = []\n\n    # 1. Summary\n    sections.append(\"## Summary\\n\")\n    sections.append(\n        f\"- **Target**: {report.target_dir}\\n\"\n        f\"- **Files analyzed**: {report.files_analyzed}\\n\"\n        f\"- **Files skipped**: {report.files_skipped}\\n\"\n        f\"- **Rollout mode**: {report.rollout_mode}\\n\"\n        f\"- **Total findings**: {len(unsuppressed)}\\n\"\n        f\"- **Blocking findings**: {blocking}\\n\"\n        f\"- **Scan duration**: {report.scan_duration_seconds:.4f}s\\n\"\n    )\n\n    # 2. Unwired Optional Callable Injections\n    sections.append(\"## Unwired Optional Callable Injections\\n\")\n    uc = [f for f in report.unwired_callables if not f.suppressed]\n    if uc:\n        for f in uc:\n            sections.append(\n                f\"- **{f.symbol_name}** ({f.file_path}:{f.line_number}) \"\n                f\"[{f.severity}]: {f.detail}\\n\"\n            )\n    else:\n        sections.append(\"No unsuppressed unwired callable findings.\\n\")\n\n    # 3. Orphan Modules / Symbols\n    sections.append(\"## Orphan Modules / Symbols\\n\")\n    om = [f for f in report.orphan_modules if not f.suppressed]\n    if om:\n        for f in om:\n            sections.append(\n                f\"- **{f.symbol_name}** ({f.file_path}:{f.line_number}) \"\n                f\"[{f.severity}]: {f.detail}\\n\"\n            )\n    else:\n        sections.append(\"No unsuppressed orphan module findings.\\n\")\n\n    # 4. Unregistered Dispatch Entries\n    sections.append(\"## Unregistered Dispatch Entries\\n\")\n    ur = [f for f in report.unwired_registries if not f.suppressed]\n    if ur:\n        for f in ur:\n            sections.append(\n                f\"- **{f.symbol_name}** ({f.file_path}:{f.line_number}) \"\n                f\"[{f.severity}]: {f.detail}\\n\"\n            )\n    else:\n        sections.append(\"No unsuppressed registry findings.\\n\")\n\n    # 5. Recommended Remediation\n    sections.append(\"## Recommended Remediation\\n\")\n    if uc:\n        sections.append(\n            \"- **Unwired callables**: Wire Optional[Callable] parameters \"\n            \"at call sites or add to whitelist if intentionally unused.\\n\"\n        )\n    if om:\n        sections.append(\n            \"- **Orphan modules**: Import orphan modules from consumer code \"\n            \"or remove if no longer needed.\\n\"\n        )\n    if ur:\n        sections.append(\n            \"- **Broken registries**: Fix registry entries to reference \"\n            \"resolvable callables or remove stale entries.\\n\"\n        )\n    if not uc and not om and not ur:\n        sections.append(\"No remediation needed — all checks pass.\\n\")\n\n    # 7. wiring are not detected.\\n\"\n        \"- Alias resolution is limited to direct name references.\\n\"\n        \"- Registry detection uses pattern matching on variable names; \"\n        \"non-conventional naming may be missed.\\n\"\n    )\n\n    # Assemble full document\n    body = \"\\n\".join(sections)\n    content = f\"---\\n{fm_yaml}---\\n\\n{body}\"\n\n return {\n            \"file_path\": self.file_path,\n            \"content_hash\": self.content_hash,\n            \"imports\": self.imports,\n            \"exports\": self.exports,\n            \"references\": self.references,\n            \"metadata\": self.metadata,\n        }\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass CacheStats:\n    \"\"\"Cache hit/miss statistics.\"\"\"\n\n    hits: int = 0\n    misses: \"hit_rate\": round(self.hit_rate, 4),\n        }\n\n\nclass ResultCache:\n    \"\"\"Content-hash keyed cache for static analysis results.\n\n    Stores results keyed by content hash. In production, AST-based\n    analysis would be plugged in via the tool parameter.\n    \"\"\"\n    lines = content.splitlines()\n    imports: list[str] = []\n    exports: list[str] = []\n\n    for line in lines:\n        stripped = line.strip()\n        # Python imports\n        if stripped.startswith(\"import \") or stripped.startswith(\"from \"):\n            imports.append(stripped)\n        # JS/TS imports\n        elif stripped.startswith(\"import \"):\n            imports.append(stripped)\n        # Python __all__\n        elif \"__all__\" in stripped:\n            exports.append(stripped)\n        # JS/TS exports\n        elif stripped.startswith(\"export \"):\n            exports.append(stripped)\n\n    return FileAnalysis(\n        file_path=file_path,\n        content_hash=compute_content_hash(content),\n        imports=imports,\n        exports=exports,\n        references=[],\n        metadata={\n            \"line_count\": len(lines),\n            \"size_bytes\": len(content),\n        },\n    )\n\n\nclass ToolOrchestrator:\n    \"\"\"Orchestrates static analysis tools per batch with caching.\n\n    Dispatches analysis for each file, using cached results when\n    content hasn't changed. Find provider directories by config.provider_dir_names convention\n    2. For each Python file in provider dirs, check if any file outside\n       the provider dir imports it\n    3. If file_references provided (dual evidence rule), also check if\n       any FileAnalysis.references mention the module — modules with\n       references but no imports are NOT flagged as orphans\n    4. If zero importers AND zero references, emit orphan_module finding\n    5. Apply exclude_patterns and whitelist suppression\n\n    Args:\n        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n        file_references: Optional mapping of file_path -> list of references\n            from FileAnalysis.references (populated by AST plugin). When\n            provided, enables dual evidence rule. When None, falls back\n            to import-graph-only evidence.\n\n    Returns:\n        List of WiringFinding with finding_type=\"orphan_module\".\n    \"\"\"\n    provider_dirs = _find_provider_dirs(source_dir, config.provider_dir_names)\n    if not provider_dirs:\n        return []\n\n    # Collect all Python files and parse them for imports\n    all_files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, [])\n    all_imports: set[str] = set()\n    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module] = {}\n\n    for f in all_files:\n        tree = _safe_parse(f)\n        if tree is not None:\n            trees[f] = tree\n\n    # Gather imports from files OUTSIDE provider directories\n    for f, tree in trees.items():\n        is_in_provider = any(\n            f.resolve().is_relative_to(pd.resolve()) for pd in provider_dirs\n        )\n        if not is_in_provider:\n            all_imports.update(_extract_imports(tree))\n\n    # Build aggregated reference set for dual evidence rule\n    all_references: set[str] = set()\n    if file_references is not None:\n        for refs in file_references.values():\n            all_references.update(refs)\n\n    dual_evidence_active = file_references is not None\n\n    findings: list[WiringFinding] = []\n\n    for provider_dir in provider_dirs:\n        for py_file in sorted(provider_dir.glob(\"*.py\")):\n            # Apply exclude patterns\n            if any(fnmatch(py_file.name, pat) for pat in config.exclude_patterns):\n                continue\n\n            # Derive the module path components\n            try:\n                rel = py_file.relative_to(source_dir)\n            except ValueError:\n                continue\n\n            # Build possible import names\n            module_stem = py_file.stem\n            module_dotpath = str(rel.with_suffix(\"\")).replace(\"/\", \".\").replace(\"\\\\\", \".\")\n\n            # Evidence 1: Check if any external file imports this module\n            is_imported = False\n            for imp in all_imports:\n                if module_dotpath in imp or module_stem in imp:\n                    is_imported = True\n                    break\n\n            if is_imported:\n                continue\n\n            # Optional[Callable] constructor parameters.\n\n    Returns list of (class_name.param_name, param_name, line_number).\n    \"\"\"\n    injectables: list[tuple[str, str, int]] = []\n\n    for node in                         (symbol, arg.arg, arg.lineno)\n                        )\n\n    return injectables\n\n\ndef _is_optional_callable(annotation: ast.expr) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if an annotation represents Optional[Callable] or Callable | None.\"\"\"\n    # Optional[Callable] -> Subscript(Name('Optional'), Name('Callable'))\n    if isinstance(annotation, ast.Subscript):\n        if isinstance(annotation.value, ast.Name) and annotation.value.id == \"Optional\":\n            slice_val = annotation.slice\n            if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Name) and slice_val.id == \"Callable\":\n                return True\n            # Optional[Callable[...]]\n            if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Subscript):\n                if isinstance(slice_val.value, ast.Name) and slice_val.value.id == \"Callable\":\n                    return True\n        # Also check Attribute form: typing.Optional\n        if isinstance(annotation.value, ast.Attribute):\n            if annotation.value.attr == \"Optional\":\n                slice_val = annotation.slice\n                if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Name) and slice_val.id == \"Callable\":\n                    return True\n\n    # Callable | None -> BinOp(Name('Callable'), BitOr, Constant(None))\n    if isinstance(annotation, ast.BinOp) and isinstance(annotation.op, ast.BitOr):\n        left, right = annotation.left, annotation.right\n        if (isinstance(left, ast.Name) and left.id == \"Callable\" and\n                isinstance(right, ast.Constant) and right.value is None):\n            return False\n\n\ndef _has_none_default(func_def: ast.FunctionDef, target_arg: ast.arg) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if the given arg has a default value of None.\"\"\"\n    args = func_def.args\n    # defaults len(all_args) - len(defaults)\n    for i, arg in enumerate(all_args):\n        if arg is target_arg:\n            default_idx = i - offset\n            if 0 <= default_idx < len(defaults):\n If zero importers, emit orphan_module finding\n    4. Apply exclude_patterns and whitelist suppression\n\n    Args:\n        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n\n    Returns:\n        List of WiringFinding with finding_type=\"orphan_module\".\n    \"\"\"\n    provider_dirs = _find_provider_dirs(source_dir, config.provider_dir_names)\n    if not provider_dirs:\n        return []\n\n    # Build possible import names\n            module_stem = py_file.stem\n            module_dotpath = str(rel.with_suffix(\"\")).replace(\"/\", \".\").replace(\"\\\\\", \".\")\n\n            # Check if any external file imports this module\n            is_imported = False\n            for imp in all_imports:\n                if module_dotpath in imp or module_stem in imp:\n                    is_imported = True\n                    break\n\n            if not is_imported:\n                findings.append(\n                    WiringFinding(\n                        finding_type=\"orphan_module\",\n                        file_path=str(py_file),\n                        symbol_name=module_dotpath,\n                        line_number=1,\n                        detail=(\n                            f\"Module '{module_dotpath}' in provider directory \"\n                            f\"'{provider_dir.name}' has zero inbound imports\"\n                        ),\n                        severity=\"major\",\n                    )\n                )\n\n    # Check module-level definitions\n    for node in ast.iter_child_nodes(tree):\n        if isinstance(node, (ast.FunctionDef, ast.AsyncFunctionDef)):\n            if node.name == name:\n                return True\n        elif isinstance(node, ast.ClassDef):\n            if node.name == name:\n                return True\n        elif isinstance(node, ast.Assign):\n            for target in node.targets:\n                if isinstance(target, ast.Name) and target.id == name:\n                    return True\n\n    # Check if importable\n    if name in all_imports:\n        return True\n\n    return False\n\n\ndef analyze_registries(\n    config: WiringConfig,\n    source_dir: Path,\n) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n    \"\"\"Detect broken dispatch registry entries referencing nonexistent callables.\n\n    Algorithm (section 5.2.3):\n    1. Scan files for module-level dict assignments matching registry patterns\n    2. For each dict entry, verify the value references an importable callable\n    3. Unresolved references emit unwired_registry findings\n\n    Args:\n        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n\n    Returns:\n        List of WiringFinding with finding_type=\"unwired_registry\".\n    \"\"\"\n    files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module] = {}\n    all_imports_by_file: dict[Path, set[str]] = {}\n\n    for f in files:\n        tree = _safe_parse(f)\n        if tree is not None:\n            trees[f] = tree\n            all_imports_by_file[f] = _extract_imports(tree)\n\n    findings: list[WiringFinding] = []\n\n    for file_path, tree in trees.items():\n        file_imports = all_imports_by_file.get(file_path, set())\n\n        for node in ast.iter_child_nodes(tree):\n            if not isinstance(node, ast.Assign):\n                continue\n\n            for target in node.targets:\n                if not isinstance(target, ast.Name):\n                    continue\n                if not _matches_registry_pattern(target.id, config.registry_patterns):\n                    continue\n\n                # This is a registry assignment — check if value is a dict\n                if not isinstance(node.value, ast.Dict):\n                    continue\n\n                for key_node, val_node in zip(node.value.keys, node.value.values):\n                    if val_node is None:\n                        continue\n\n                    # Explicit None is allowed\n                    if isinstance(val_node, ast.Constant) and val_node.value is None:\n                        continue\n\n                    # Name reference — must be resolvable\n                    if isinstance(val_node, ast.Name):\n                        if not _resolve_name_in_scope(\n                            val_node.id, tree, file_imports\n                        ):\n                            key_repr = (\n                                ast.literal_eval(key_node)\n                                if isinstance(key_node, ast.Constant)\n                                else \"<dynamic>\"\n                            )\n                            findings.append(\n                                WiringFinding(\n                                    finding_type=\"unwired_registry\",\n                                    file_path=str(file_path),\n                                    symbol_name=f\"{target.id}[{key_repr!r}]\",\n                                    line_number=val_node.lineno,\n                                    detail=(\n                                        f\"Registry '{target.id}' entry \"\n                                        f\"'{key_repr}' references unresolvable \"\n                                        f\"callable '{val_node.id}'\"\n                                    ),\n                                    severity=\"critical\",\n                                )\n                            )\n\n                    # String reference — try to resolve as dotted path\n                    elif isinstance(val_node, ast.Constant) and isinstance(\n                        val_node.value, str\n                    ):\n                        ref = val_node.value\n                        parts = ref.rsplit(\".\", 1)\n                        func_name = parts[-1] if len(parts) > 1 else ref\n                        if not _resolve_name_in_scope(\n                            func_name, tree, file_imports\n                        ):\n                            key_repr = (\n                                ast.literal_eval(key_node)\n                                if isinstance(key_node, ast.Constant)\n                                else \"<dynamic>\"\n                            )\n                            findings.append(\n                                WiringFinding(\n                                    finding_type=\"unwired_registry\",\n                                    file_path=str(file_path),\n                                    symbol_name=f\"{target.id}[{key_repr!r}]\",\n                                    line_number=val_node.lineno,\n                                    detail=(\n                                        f\"Registry '{target.id}' entry \"\n                                        f\"'{key_repr}' references unresolvable \"\n                                        f\"string path '{ref}'\"\n                                    ),\n                                    severity=\"critical\",\n                                )\n                            )\n\n    # Apply whitelist\n    whitelist = load_whitelist(config.whitelist_path, config.rollout_mode)\n    return _apply_whitelist(findings, whitelist)\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Top-level entry point\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef run_wiring_analysis(\n    config: WiringConfig,\n    source_dir: Path,\n) -> WiringReport:\n    \"\"\"Run all three wiring analyzers and produce a WiringReport.\n\n    Args:\n        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n\n    Returns:\n        WiringReport aggregating findings from all analyzers.\n    \"\"\"\n    start = time.monotonic()\n\n    _, skipped = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n    files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n    files_analyzed = len(files)\n\n    unwired = analyze_unwired_callables(config, source_dir)\n    orphans = analyze_orphan_modules(config, source_dir)\n    registries = analyze_registries(config, source_dir)\n\n    duration = time.monotonic() - start\n\n    return WiringReport(\n        target_dir=str(source_dir),\n        files_analyzed=files_analyzed,\n        files_skipped=skipped,\n        unwired_callables=unwired,\n        orphan_modules=orphans,\n        unwired_registries=registries,\n        scan_duration_seconds=round(duration, 4),\n        rollout_mode=config.rollout_mode,\n    )\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Report emission (section 5.4)\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef emit_report(report: WiringReport, output_path: Path) -> Path:\n    \"\"\"Write a wiring verification report with YAML frontmatter and 7 Markdown sections.\n\n    Frontmatter contains 16 fields per section 5.6. String fields are serialized\n    with yaml.safe_dump() to prevent YAML injection (section 5.4).\n\n    Args:\n        report: Aggregated wiring analysis report.\n        output_path: Destination file path.\n\n    Returns:\n        The output_path after writing.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Compute severity counts from unsuppressed findings\n    unsuppressed = report.unsuppressed_findings\n    critical_count = sum(1 for f in unsuppressed if f.severity == \"critical\")\n    major_count = sum(1 for f in unsuppressed if f.severity == \"major\")\n    info_count = sum(1 for f in unsuppressed if f.severity == \"info\")\n    suppressed_count = sum(1 for f in report.all_findings if f.suppressed)\n\n    # blocking_findings depends on rollout_mode\n    blocking = report.blocking_count()\n\n    # Build frontmatter dict (16 fields per section 5.6)\n    fm: dict = {\n        \"gate\": \"wiring-verification\",\n        \"target_dir\": report.target_dir,\n        \"files_analyzed\": report.files_analyzed,\n        \"files_skipped\": report.files_skipped,\n        \"rollout_mode\": report.rollout_mode,\n        \"analysis_complete\": True,\n        \"audit_artifacts_used\": 0,\n        \"unwired_callable_count\": len([\n            f for f in report.unwired_callables if not f.suppressed\n        ]),\n        \"orphan_module_count\": len([\n            f for f in report.orphan_modules if not f.suppressed\n        ]),\n        \"unwired_registry_count\": len([\n            f for f in report.unwired_registries if not f.suppressed\n        ]),\n        \"critical_count\": critical_count,\n        \"major_count\": major_count,\n        \"info_count\": info_count,\n        \"total_findings\": len(unsuppressed),\n        \"blocking_findings\": blocking,\n        \"whitelist_entries_applied\": suppressed_count,\n    }\n\n    # Serialize frontmatter with yaml.safe_dump for string safety\n    fm_yaml = yaml.safe_dump(fm, default_flow_style=False, sort_keys=False)\n\n    # Build Markdown body with 7 sections (section 5.4.1)\n    sections: list[str] = []\n\n    # 1. Summary\n    sections.append(\"## Summary\\n\")\n    sections.append(\n        f\"- **Target**: {report.target_dir}\\n\"\n        f\"- **Files analyzed**: {report.files_analyzed}\\n\"\n        f\"- **Files skipped**: {report.files_skipped}\\n\"\n        f\"- **Rollout mode**: {report.rollout_mode}\\n\"\n        f\"- **Total findings**: {len(unsuppressed)}\\n\"\n        f\"- **Blocking findings**: {blocking}\\n\"\n        f\"- **Scan duration**: {report.scan_duration_seconds:.4f}s\\n\"\n    )\n\n    # 2. Unwired Optional Callable Injections\n    sections.append(\"## Unwired Optional Callable Injections\\n\")\n    uc = [f for f in report.unwired_callables if not f.suppressed]\n    if uc:\n        for f in uc:\n            sections.append(\n                f\"- **{f.symbol_name}** ({f.file_path}:{f.line_number}) \"\n                f\"[{f.severity}]: {f.detail}\\n\"\n            )\n    else:\n        sections.append(\"No unsuppressed unwired callable findings.\\n\")\n\n    # 3. Orphan Modules / Symbols\n    sections.append(\"## Orphan Modules / Symbols\\n\")\n    om = [f for f in report.orphan_modules if not f.suppressed]\n    if om:\n        for f in om:\n            sections.append(\n                f\"- **{f.symbol_name}** ({f.file_path}:{f.line_number}) \"\n                f\"[{f.severity}]: {f.detail}\\n\"\n            )\n    else:\n        sections.append(\"No unsuppressed orphan module findings.\\n\")\n\n    # 4. Recommended Remediation\n    sections.append(\"## Recommended Remediation\\n\")\n    if uc:\n        sections.append(\n            \"- **Unwired callables**: Wire Optional[Callable] parameters \"\n            \"at call sites or add to whitelist if intentionally unused.\\n\"\n        )\n    if om:\n        sections.append(\n            \"- **Orphan modules**: Import orphan modules from consumer code \"\n            \"or remove if no longer needed.\\n\"\n        )\n    if ur:\n        sections.append(\n            \"- **Broken registries**: Fix registry entries to reference \"\n            \"resolvable callables or remove stale entries.\\n\"\n        )\n    if not uc and not om and not ur:\n        sections.append(\"No remediation needed — all checks pass.\\n\")\n\n    # 7. wiring are not detected.\\n\"\n        \"- Alias resolution is limited to direct name references.\\n\"\n        \"- Registry detection uses pattern matching on variable names; \"\n        \"non-conventional naming may be missed.\\n\"\n    )\n\n    # Assemble full document\n    body = \"\\n\".join(sections)\n    content = f\"---\\n{fm_yaml}---\\n\\n{body}\"\n\n
